Besides, AX-ZIP Extractor is simple and convenient file manager.\r\n\r\nMain Features\r\n\r\nExtraction from ZIP, CAB, RAR, JAR, XAP, GZIP, BZIP2, XZ, TAR and 7Z archives.\r\nExtraction from ISO images (ISO 9660 and ISO 13346 \"UDF\").\r\nSimultaneous work with several archives.\r\nOne drag extraction of files from archive.\r\nSearch of archives and files within the archives.\r\nBookmarks for archives and files in the archives.\r\nSupport of cloud drives and special folders.\r\nSupport of main file manager functions.\r\nSupport of drag and drop technology.\r\nDisplay of archive structure as a tree.\r\nFamiliar Explorer-like user interface.\r\n\r\nOverview\r\n\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor utility views ZIP archives and archives of other types as folders containing folders and files whose structure is shown as a tree. up to the maximum hand limit on each hand.\r\n\r\nOnline Blackjack Tutorial\r\n\r\nThe main aim of this table game classic is for you to create a hand that totals more than the dealer’s hand but without going over 21. You commence the game by first placing a bet. Cards are dealt in rotation from left to right starting from the Dealer. The dealer’s hand will have one card face up and another face down. If your card totals closer to 21 and is more than the Dealer’s hand, then you win.\r\n\r\nSplit\r\n\r\nWhen your hands consists of two of the same cards, you have the option to split. This doesn’t apply to Aces but by splitting your hand, you can also double your initial bet.\r\n\r\nDouble Down\r\n\r\nAfter you have seen your initial two hands, you can double your bet to increase your profit. Following a Double Down, you only get one extra card to complete your hand. You can also double down after a split.\r\n\r\nBlackJack Game Rules:\r\n\r\n- Blackjack is played with 3 boxes and 6 standard decks of 52 cards (Jokers not included).\r\n- The object of the game is to create a hand with a value that is equal to or closer to 21 than the dealer’s hand without going over.\r\n- Number cards (2-10) count as a face value, Aces count as either 1 or 11, and Kings, Queens, and Jacks count as 10.\r\n- No particular significance is given to any of the 4 suits.\r\n- Play takes place against a computerized dealer. The dealer is dealt two cards, and the player is dealt two cards in each box. \r\n- The player’s cards are dealt face up, while only the dealer’s first card is shown.\r\n- You can decide to Hit, Double, Split, or Stand.\r\n- Depending on your cards and the dealer’s card, you may additionally have the options to split, take even money or take insurance.\r\n- If you decide to Hit, Double, or Split, the next card or cards dealt are counted toward those decisions.\r\n- When you decide to Stand, or your hand bursts, the next cards dealt are automatically assigned to the next hand or the dealer’s hand depending on which hand you are playing.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NXB4M7QVMM8","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Twilight by Chad Copeland","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.51560.14433039802010393.b6449664-92eb-42be-b030-34a4a7548f4c.fd127d5a-823e-43a9-aa83-95b1f7d68886","Height":150,"Width":150,"BackgroundColor":"transparent","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"ຟຼີ(ຟຼີ)","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["Microsoft.TwilightbyChadCopeland_8wekyb3d8bbwe"],"ContentIds":["6041aa1c-a236-fff9-5e58-7e7b7a626936"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"A leading figure in the use of aerial drones, Copeland offers up gorgeous photos from around the world, taken at sunrise or sunset.
